< Text>
Where to start if you're bringing in an empty trailer when you make the right on shoemaker you need to take the first right which is performance teams drop yard, don't bring it to the warehouse they will tell you to turn around and take it to the drop yard.

I also find it interesting that at the drop yard they ask you for your license you're dropping a trailer !!! Then when you come to the warehouse they ask you at the gate for your license when you go in to pick up your bills they ask you at the window for your license and after you pick up your trailer to exit they ask you again for your drivers license that's four times what do you need all this information for and what do you do with it after you collect it I think it's a little ridiculous...... Make sure you have all your information you need prior to coming to performance teams warehouse,,,, I find that the people that work here don't really care to help anybody and trying to get information is like pulling teeth but probably pulling teeth is less painful than dealing with these people good luck and happy travels !!!!< /Text>

<Rate>5<//Rate><UserId.>110178760489961873417</UserId.>< review>
What a wonderful surprise to find this gem of a place. I was tasked to bring some meats to bbq and found La Pradera Carniceria. LPC not only offers the varieties of marinated meats but at the excellent price. I got their marinated flap meat and chicken, 3 lbs each. I also picked up red and green salsa along with guacamole. I also happy to pick up this brand of street taco style tortillas that I didn't see in usual supermarkets. Both meats were easy to cook and came out perfectly off the grill. I simply diced up the meat nicely and spread them with condiments for the DIY street taco.< /review>

<userid>115420862901792645501<//userid><Name>Francis Basco< /Name><time>1478189713439<//time><Rate>4<//Rate>< review>
When I went in, the place was kinda dimly  and kinda silent when entering.

They have small cupcakes as examples but entire display case that was empty so I wasn't sure if I had to order earlier. Apparently all their stock is in the back.

Despite all this. Their cupcakes  are really good. The service was quick and the price was cheap.

I love cupcake shops and while this place was a little more lax rather than the more pop-y vibe you get from other cupcake places, the taste of the cupcakes more than made up for it.<//review>

< review>
BikeBling has been a fantastic outfit to purchase from.  The main reason is customer support and personal care after purchase, not to mention highly competitive pricing.  I have recommended friends and colleagues to them who have had the same experience.

< Review>
I've bought things online and in person at the store without issues but their business model has finally caught up with them. Offering items for online purchase that are not in inventory was OK in 2010 but not today, particularly in the current covid-induced bicycle industry frenzy where so many items are simply sold out from vendors and not currently available.

Here is what happened: I placed an order without ensuring it was "in inventory" and did the waiting game like others have explained, (1) waiting for an "order has shipped" and tracking number email, (2) contacting them by email (2 times over 2 weeks) and  eventually getting a response explaining they are "expecting shipment from the vendor," (3) doing it again a week later and getting a similar response, (4) finally reaching out to the vendor to find out they have none in stock and can't provide an ETA on shipment of the item to any dealers, (5) calling Bike Bling but never able to speak with anyone to cancel the order. (6) Eventually I received a return call from a woman at BB that was very pleasant and she cancelled my order without issue.

I like this shop and will shop there again at some point but they really need to step into this decade and stop this business practice. As the reviews indicate, they are killing their reputation and business.</Review>

<Review>While reading this review, please keep in mind that my order was placed and fulfilled between July and August 2020, at a height of the COVID-19 pandemic, when bicycle stores were pummeled, demand for bicycles and service had skyrocketed, cheap and medium priced bikes from reputable brands were scarcely available, and fulfillment and service took weeks.

I placed an order for a lower end electric road bike toward the end of July. I was contacted by email a couple of times and asked to call Kerry to discuss. I requested email correspondence due to trouble with phone communication, but my email messages received only canned automated responses. The issue ended up not being discussed, but I assume it had to do with the bike I ordered being unavailable, since the bike I ended up received was a higher end model with upgraded components. My order arrived 16 days after it was placed, which, under the circumstances, was better than I expected. On the other hand, although professional assembly and adjustments were included in the price, the bike needed work on top of the simple assembly, including brake bleeding, issues with rotor rubbing, rear derailleur adjustments, etc. With bike shops in my area not accepting service work for 2-3 weeks, I had to order a bleed kit and tools, and attempt to perform the work myself. After endlessly watching youtube tutorials and several hours attempting to correct the issues, the bike now is at an acceptable state to be ridden. Fine tuning at a bike store will have to wait until after demand subsides.

I understand the frustration of customers not getting answers about their orders and having to wait long periods of time. It is obvious to me that the bikebling website is not integrated with their inventory database and the items shown on the website are not necessarily in stock. Case in point, the unavailable bike I ordered is still listed on their website as available in every possible size and color!

I personally was pleased with my order, which was received in a very reasonable time frame given the circumstances, and at a price that is several hundreds of dollars lower than anything offered from elsewhere these days. Even with the extra work I put and materials I had to purchase, it was definitely worth it. Whether such a benefit/hassle ratio is acceptable to you is for you to decide.< /Review><gmapID>0x80dbf483a52a4a35:0xdcbb319f75c327b3< /gmapID><response>None<//response><username>papamicd0< /username>< time>

<Text>I have flipped my opinion on BikeBling as they have done right by me since my original post.  My original posting was written on the same day my last email to BikeBling was seemingly rebuffed by an automated response.  That email contained wording expressing my frustration similar to my original post.  A day later I received a very apologetic email from BikeBling and a commitment to ship the part of my order that had been in stock.  As it turns out, 1 of 2 rotors, 1 of 2 adapters, and the bleed kit were back-ordered keeping the order on hold.  The rest of the brake set parts were in hand and were shipped to me within a few days.  While all I really wanted was an update, I appreciate and acknowledge the effort their team put in to make things better.  While I still have to wait for the last of the parts, I choose to attribute the delays to these odd times we're living in and the incredible run on bikes and bike parts it has created.  I'm not sure how long the rear brake set will hold up, but I was able to service the failed front set.  I'm still riding and feel reassured that the BikeBling team is doing what they can to keep it that way.

My original post:
"This place has terrible customer service.  I placed an order online 3 weeks ago and have heard nothing from them since my order confirmation.  I can go into the store now that things have reopened, but I would have to carve a few hours out of my day to make the trip from down by the bay up to escondido. < text>
I ordered a Bell Super DH helmet from their website.  The transaction and overall experience has been quite smooth.  The helmet was backordered, and the only reason I deducted a star was for the ambiguity of how that was conveyed on the webpage.   It says "ships in 1-3 days".  After reading other reviews this can also mean out of stock.

Having not heard from them in the 3 day window I reached out to customer service via email and much to my surprise, I received a reply on a Saturday evening.   This put me in good spirits.

Once I received the helmet everything was as expected.

They were not able to provide parts but even went as far as to offer a very gracious discount on another helmet.

Needles to say, I will be a returning customer from across the country,  and I would highly recommend them to any rider out there.   I will spread these good praises at my enduro races as well.<//text>

The walls are covered, floor to ceiling, with an endless variety of gear, bikes, accessories, etc. I could waste hours of my life in this store just looking around at stuff I don't even need. If you need something, chances are this store is gonna have it. The prices are pretty competitive too. If that's all you care about, this is the store for you; if you care about customer service, see below for the "cons" section.

Cons:
I have been in this store 5 or 6 times in the past 6 months, and an employee has offered help only once. Most of the employees here don't realize you exist unless you're at the checkout with your wallet in your hand. The one employee who did help me was actually great, and I wish I knew his name so I could drop it here. The few times I actually asked for help from other employees, I was treated as a nuisance, help was minimal, and felt hustled to the checkout. Even one time my family was in town and we came in after walking Grand Ave and my mom commented on the poor service!

I was in there today for about 45min trying on/looking for a new pair of clipless shoes. No one ever said "hello," "goodbye," or anything at all to me while I was there. They had the shoes and size I wanted, but I walked out, called Bicycle Warehouse in Escondido and asked if they could order the shoes. I'll have to wait for my shoes, but the superior service is worth the wait.

I want to give this store a 2/5, but the one employee who acknowledged my existence gets it an extra star.</Review>< Pics>

<review>So here's my experience with this shop. All totally internet based. The reality I have learned is that when you order something online you have to be patient. I ordered a 2018 bell super DH for my son to have on our MTB trip. They did not have the color we picked initially. Terry from bike bling emailed me informing me that they did not have the color we had picked. He asked if we wanted to get a 2019 color instead and needles to say we were ecstatic about getting to pick a new color for the same price of the sale helmets. We went back and forward because the 2019 colors were also limited. (this was a little frustrating) Though Terry was never rude his responses were short and direct yet had all the information I needed to satisfy me. a day went by and still no shipping notification. I emailed Terry to ask what was going on and he mentioned to me that the helmet would ship early next week. Man I thought, bummed a little at first I was still so excited about getting a 2019 color I didn't even think to ask why would it take so long to ship my helmet. Monday comes around and again I email Terry asking about when my helmet would ship, I also let him know we had a trip planned and that I really needed it. He replied the helmet was still on its way from Bell to him and it would go for sure Wed. or Thurs. He did also offer to get me a different color they had there at the shop already shipped that day. okay, I thought this is enough. I was beginning to get worried I might not get my helmet in time for my trip. After my wife calmed me down and talked some sense into me, I asked Terry one last question. would my helmet get here before my trip? he replied quickly that it would. later that day I got my shipping notification that my helmet was on its way. Moral of the story, if your'e used to the wicked fast shipping of Amazon and no patience I would not recommend this place. but if you want a great deal on a product, good customer service, fast email response to questions then this is the store for you. < username>
Walter Macalma<//username>
<date>1402703755936< /date>< Rate>
4</Rate>
<Text>You better bring the plastic. If you're not careful, and few cyclists are.....with their wallets, that is. You could spend a bikesworth on clothing and gear, or heck walk out with a $15K bike. Among my group of friends we mainly come for a few key items like swiftiwck socks, capo/nalini gear or road shoes, but the real draw here is the mountain bike part of the store.

Remember this place is called Bike bling and not road bling or bmx bling, so they offer a large selection of everything, but compared to other shops the mountain bike portions are most impressive. Granted I don't ride dirt doesn't mean I don't know the gear when I see it. Easily 2-3 times the selection and inventory of any other mountain bike shop in North County..

It can be overwhelming because of how stacked on top of things the selection is. Like walking in and feeling like the bikes are coming down on you. You don't really get a really good look at them while on the racks. The helmet selection is kind of small and literally tucked away in the corner, while the mountain bike helmet section is wide open. Tri stuff is all over the place, but logically split between mens and women, solid womens Castelli selection which is rare. Trainers could be more clearly marked and displayed, nutrition is just a central isle without much thought given to display. Large work area has bikes being worked on all the time by the expert mechanics. The real gems are up on the wall behind the counter and of course they keep the higher end upgrade drivetrain, electronics and componentry out of reach.

Service on sales for the bikes is excellent, someone will always greet you when they see you looking at the bikes. Service from the mechanical department is amazing when it comes to workmanship. Fast, accurate, reliable. In the rock climbing world the term "spray" is something I would describe the staff overall. Always hyping and amping up the latest and greatest even if out of your price range. They don't carry anything low end and not much on sale, but for those that want the good stuff, you come here.

I would not suggest coming her to buy your first bike or a childs bike. The name implies a certain level of elitism which few people buying their first bike or their kid a bike need. Part of the elitist mentaility brings a high level of craftsmanship and quality, probably above and beyond intention, so that's nice. Their biggest weakness as with most shops is tri gear, but since bike is only 1/3 of the tri discipline that is understandable. Parking can be difficult and their fitting rooms are small, not much room to maneuver while shopping. Overall this place can be a nightmare or heaven and to me I'm closer to the latter.</Text>< pictures>

1 taco de carne asada

I trusted the cook to complete my order.

Unfortunately upon arriving home, I was missing 1 of my Chile‚Äôs Rellenos.

I would give a 5 star review if my order was complete.

They seemed to have a new twist on old favorites and some new dishes I plan to come back for. I chose the 5 tacos to try 5 different meats and each was excellent - so fresh, so clean and so delicious: Pastor, Carnitas, Shrimp, Salmon and Lengua served with a green grilled onion, grilled jalape√±o and radish slices. I have nothing but positive things to say about the team over Kinetic Society. I was originally interested in picking up a couple jerseys to rep my fraternity at music festivals, so I submitted a form to customize the jerseys. Within 30 minutes of submitting it, Bryant called me up and took the time to talk to me about the specifics of our design and worked with me to come up with a few mock ups of designs that he thought we would like. After exchanging a couple ideas back and forth, Bryant was more than happy to work with us to create a design that everyone in my chapter liked. We promptly placed a larger order of jerseys....much larger than initially anticipated because everyone liked the design. Despite this larger order, we were able to get our jerseys in an extremely timely manner and the order turned out flawless. The jerseys are fire, and the experience of working with Bryant and the team over at Kinetic Society made this order top tier. We will be contacting them for future orders because it was a pleasure working with them and they know how to make clean designs.

UPDATE: Now that Covid is finally done, and restrictions are lifted, festival season is back. Kinetic society was the first group that popped up in my mind to get another custom set of jerseys. Upon doing so, I was met with the same personal level of customer service. I worked with their rep, where I chose a design that I liked but made modifications on. Everytime I wanted to try out a design, he would send back a mock up. The ordering process was super easy, and I've been kept in the loop the entire time, so I don't have to worry about my order status. I look forward to place even more orders with them.< /Text>
